## Manipulation and Interaction with Objects

**Domain:** Physical  
**Subdomain:** Manipulation and Interaction with Objects

### Scenario 1: Tool Use and Instrumental Manipulation

**Description:** In this scenario, a #ToolUser selects #ManipulationTools to perform #InstrumentalActions on #TargetObjects, applying #ControlledForces to achieve #ManipulationGoals. The process requires understanding #ToolAffordances, #ForceApplication techniques, and #ObjectResponses to use tools effectively.


**Elements:**

- **ToolUser** (Entity): Person employing instruments to manipulate objects
- **ManipulationTools** (Entity): Instruments that extend or modify human manipulation capabilities
- **InstrumentalActions** (Process): Purposeful activities using tools to affect objects
- **TargetObjects** (Entity): Items being manipulated through tool use
- **ControlledForces** (Entity): Directed energy applied through tools
- **ManipulationGoals** (Entity): Intended outcomes of tool-mediated actions
- **ToolAffordances** (Quality): Functional possibilities offered by specific tools
- **ForceApplication** (Process): Methods of directing energy through tools
- **ObjectResponses** (Quality): How target objects react to tool-mediated forces

**Relations:**

- ToolUser selects ManipulationTools based on ToolAffordances
- ToolUser performs InstrumentalActions on TargetObjects
- InstrumentalActions involve ForceApplication through ManipulationTools
- ControlledForces are directed toward achieving ManipulationGoals
- TargetObjects exhibit ObjectResponses to applied forces
- ToolAffordances determine possible InstrumentalActions
- ManipulationGoals guide selection of ManipulationTools and ForceApplication methods

### Scenario 2: Object Assembly and Construction Activities

**Description:** In this scenario, a #Constructor combines #ComponentObjects using #JoiningMethods to create #CompositeStructures. The process involves understanding #StructuralRelationships, #AssemblySequences, and #ConnectionTypes to build stable and functional constructions.


**Elements:**

- **Constructor** (Entity): Person assembling objects into larger structures
- **ComponentObjects** (Entity): Individual parts used in construction
- **JoiningMethods** (Process): Techniques for connecting components together
- **CompositeStructures** (Entity): Assembled constructions made from multiple components
- **StructuralRelationships** (Relation): Connections and dependencies between components
- **AssemblySequences** (Process): Ordered steps in construction process
- **ConnectionTypes** (Quality): Different ways components can be joined or attached

**Relations:**

- Constructor combines ComponentObjects using JoiningMethods
- JoiningMethods create StructuralRelationships between ComponentObjects
- Constructor follows AssemblySequences to build CompositeStructures
- StructuralRelationships determine stability of CompositeStructures
- ConnectionTypes define how ComponentObjects interface with each other
- AssemblySequences optimize efficiency and structural integrity
- CompositeStructures exhibit properties different from individual ComponentObjects

### Scenario 3: Precision Control and Fine Motor Manipulation

**Description:** In this scenario, a #PrecisionOperator performs #FineMotorActions requiring #ExactControl and #DelicateManipulation of #SensitiveObjects. The process demands #CoordinatedMovements, #SensoryFeedback, and #MotorAdjustments to achieve #PrecisionOutcomes.


**Elements:**

- **PrecisionOperator** (Entity): Person performing controlled, delicate manipulations
- **FineMotorActions** (Process): Small-scale, precise movements requiring high control
- **ExactControl** (Quality): High degree of accuracy in movement and force application
- **DelicateManipulation** (Process): Careful handling of fragile or sensitive objects
- **SensitiveObjects** (Entity): Items requiring gentle or precise handling
- **CoordinatedMovements** (Process): Synchronized motor actions involving multiple body parts
- **SensoryFeedback** (Entity): Visual, tactile, and proprioceptive information guiding movements
- **MotorAdjustments** (Process): Real-time corrections to movement based on feedback
- **PrecisionOutcomes** (State): Successfully achieved results requiring exact control

**Relations:**

- PrecisionOperator performs FineMotorActions on SensitiveObjects
- FineMotorActions require ExactControl and DelicateManipulation
- PrecisionOperator uses CoordinatedMovements guided by SensoryFeedback
- SensoryFeedback enables MotorAdjustments during manipulation
- MotorAdjustments maintain ExactControl throughout FineMotorActions
- DelicateManipulation prevents damage to SensitiveObjects
- CoordinatedMovements achieve intended PrecisionOutcomes

### Scenario 4: Material Shaping and Craft Manipulation

**Description:** In this scenario, a #Craftsperson uses #ShapingTechniques and #CraftingTools to perform #MaterialShaping on #WorkpieceMaterials, creating #DesiredForms through #ArtisanalProcesses. The craftsperson applies #SkilledManipulation and #CraftKnowledge while managing #MaterialProperties and #ShapingConstraints to achieve #CraftedProducts.

**Elements:**

- **Craftsperson** (Entity): Skilled person shaping materials into desired forms
- **ShapingTechniques** (Process): Specialized methods for forming and molding materials
- **CraftingTools** (Entity): Specialized instruments for material shaping
- **MaterialShaping** (Process): Transformation of raw materials into specific forms
- **WorkpieceMaterials** (Entity): Raw materials being shaped into products
- **DesiredForms** (Entity): Intended shapes or configurations for finished products
- **ArtisanalProcesses** (Process): Traditional or skilled methods of material working
- **SkilledManipulation** (Process): Expert handling requiring training and experience
- **CraftKnowledge** (Entity): Understanding of materials, tools, and techniques
- **MaterialProperties** (Quality): Characteristics affecting how materials can be shaped
- **ShapingConstraints** (Quality): Limitations imposed by materials or tools
- **CraftedProducts** (Entity): Finished items created through shaping processes

**Relations:**

- Craftsperson uses ShapingTechniques and CraftingTools for MaterialShaping
- MaterialShaping transforms WorkpieceMaterials into DesiredForms
- ArtisanalProcesses require SkilledManipulation and CraftKnowledge
- CraftKnowledge includes understanding of MaterialProperties
- MaterialProperties create ShapingConstraints
- Craftsperson works within ShapingConstraints
- Successful MaterialShaping produces CraftedProducts

### Scenario 5: Force Distribution and Load Management

**Description:** In this scenario, a #LoadManager distributes #AppliedForces across #SupportStructures and #LoadBearingElements to manage #WeightDistribution and #ForceTransmission. The manager analyzes #LoadPaths, #StressDistribution, and #StructuralStability while considering #SupportCapacity and #LoadLimits to ensure #StructuralIntegrity.

**Elements:**

- **LoadManager** (Entity): Person managing weight and force distribution in structures
- **AppliedForces** (Entity): External pressures, weights, or loads acting on structures
- **SupportStructures** (Entity): Elements designed to bear and distribute loads
- **LoadBearingElements** (Entity): Specific components that carry structural loads
- **WeightDistribution** (Process): Spreading loads across multiple support points
- **ForceTransmission** (Process): Transfer of forces through structural elements
- **LoadPaths** (Entity): Routes through which forces travel in structures
- **StressDistribution** (State): Pattern of force concentration across materials
- **StructuralStability** (Quality): Ability of structure to maintain position under load
- **SupportCapacity** (Quality): Maximum load that structural elements can bear
- **LoadLimits** (Quality): Boundaries of safe loading for structural systems
- **StructuralIntegrity** (State): Overall soundness and safety of load-bearing systems

**Relations:**

- LoadManager distributes AppliedForces across SupportStructures
- SupportStructures include LoadBearingElements for WeightDistribution
- ForceTransmission occurs through LoadPaths in structures
- WeightDistribution creates StressDistribution patterns
- LoadManager analyzes StructuralStability under various loads
- SupportCapacity determines LoadLimits for structural elements
- Proper force management maintains StructuralIntegrity


# Psychological Domain

## Emotions and Affective States

**Domain:** Psychological  
**Subdomain:** Emotions and Affective States

### Scenario 1: Emotional Recognition and Expression

**Description:** In this scenario, an #EmotionalSubject experiences #EmotionalStates triggered by #EmotionalStimuli. The subject exhibits #EmotionalExpressions through #BodyLanguage and #VocalPatterns, which are interpreted by #SocialObservers through #EmotionalRecognition processes that may lead to #SocialResponses.


**Elements:**

- **EmotionalSubject** (Entity): Person experiencing emotional states
- **EmotionalStates** (State): Internal affective conditions like joy, anger, fear, sadness
- **EmotionalStimuli** (Entity): Events, objects, or situations that trigger emotions
- **EmotionalExpressions** (Event/Process): Outward manifestations of internal emotional states
- **BodyLanguage** (Entity): Postures, gestures, and facial expressions conveying emotion
- **VocalPatterns** (Entity): Tone, pitch, and rhythm changes expressing emotion
- **SocialObservers** (Entity): People interpreting others' emotional expressions
- **EmotionalRecognition** (Event/Process): Identifying emotions in others through observation
- **SocialResponses** (Event/Process): Behavioral reactions to perceived emotions

**Relations:**

- EmotionalStimuli trigger EmotionalStates in EmotionalSubject
- EmotionalStates generate EmotionalExpressions
- EmotionalExpressions manifest through BodyLanguage and VocalPatterns
- SocialObservers perform EmotionalRecognition of EmotionalExpressions
- EmotionalRecognition leads to SocialResponses
- SocialResponses may become EmotionalStimuli for EmotionalSubject

### Scenario 2: Emotional Regulation and Coping

**Description:** In this scenario, an #Individual experiences #IntenseEmotions that may be #Disruptive to their functioning. The Individual employs #RegulationStrategies such as #CognitiveReappraisal, #EmotionalSuppression, or #SeekingSupport to achieve #EmotionalBalance and maintain #AdaptiveFunctioning.


**Elements:**

- **Individual** (Entity): Person managing their emotional responses
- **IntenseEmotions** (State): Strong affective states that may impair functioning
- **Disruptive** (Quality): Characteristic of emotions that interfere with normal activities
- **RegulationStrategies** (Event/Process): Techniques used to modify emotional responses
- **CognitiveReappraisal** (Event/Process): Changing interpretation of emotional situations
- **EmotionalSuppression** (Event/Process): Deliberately inhibiting emotional expression
- **SeekingSupport** (Event/Process): Requesting help from others for emotional management
- **EmotionalBalance** (State): Stable, manageable level of emotional intensity
- **AdaptiveFunctioning** (State): Effective performance in daily activities despite emotions

**Relations:**

- Individual experiences IntenseEmotions
- IntenseEmotions may be Disruptive to functioning
- Individual employs RegulationStrategies to manage IntenseEmotions
- RegulationStrategies include CognitiveReappraisal, EmotionalSuppression, SeekingSupport
- Successful RegulationStrategies lead to EmotionalBalance
- EmotionalBalance enables AdaptiveFunctioning

### Scenario 3: Emotional Memory and Associations

**Description:** In this scenario, a #Person encounters #MemoryTriggers that activate #EmotionalMemories associated with #PastExperiences. This creates #EmotionalReactivation of previous feelings, which may influence current #DecisionMaking and #BehavioralChoices through #AffectiveInfluence on cognitive processes.


**Elements:**

- **Person** (Entity): Individual experiencing emotional memory activation
- **MemoryTriggers** (Entity): Environmental cues that activate emotional memories
- **EmotionalMemories** (Entity): Stored associations between experiences and emotions
- **PastExperiences** (Entity): Previous events that created emotional associations
- **EmotionalReactivation** (Event/Process): Re-experiencing emotions from previous experiences
- **DecisionMaking** (Event/Process): Current choice processes influenced by emotional memories
- **BehavioralChoices** (Entity): Actions selected based on current decision-making
- **AffectiveInfluence** (Relation): Impact of emotions on cognitive and behavioral processes

**Relations:**

- MemoryTriggers activate EmotionalMemories
- EmotionalMemories connected to PastExperiences
- EmotionalMemories create EmotionalReactivation
- EmotionalReactivation exerts AffectiveInfluence on DecisionMaking
- DecisionMaking determines BehavioralChoices
- BehavioralChoices may create new MemoryTriggers

### Scenario 4: Emotional Contagion and Interpersonal Affect

**Description:** In this scenario, an #EmotionReceiver experiences #EmotionalContagion when exposed to #OthersEmotions through #SocialInteraction. The receiver undergoes #AutomaticMimicry and #EmotionalSynchronization, leading to #SharedEmotionalStates and #CollectiveAffect that create #EmotionalResonance and #GroupEmotionalDynamics.

**Elements:**

- **EmotionReceiver** (Entity): Person susceptible to catching emotions from others
- **EmotionalContagion** (Process): Automatic spreading of emotions between people
- **OthersEmotions** (Entity): Emotional states displayed by other people in social settings
- **SocialInteraction** (Process): Direct or indirect contact with emotionally expressive others
- **AutomaticMimicry** (Process): Unconscious copying of emotional expressions and behaviors
- **EmotionalSynchronization** (Process): Alignment of emotional states between individuals
- **SharedEmotionalStates** (State): Common emotional experiences across multiple people
- **CollectiveAffect** (State): Group-level emotional atmosphere or mood
- **EmotionalResonance** (Quality): Degree of emotional connection and mutual influence
- **GroupEmotionalDynamics** (Process): Collective emotional patterns and interactions

**Relations:**

- EmotionReceiver exposed to OthersEmotions through SocialInteraction
- SocialInteraction triggers EmotionalContagion process
- EmotionalContagion involves AutomaticMimicry of emotional expressions
- AutomaticMimicry leads to EmotionalSynchronization
- EmotionalSynchronization creates SharedEmotionalStates
- SharedEmotionalStates contribute to CollectiveAffect
- EmotionalResonance determines strength of EmotionalContagion
- CollectiveAffect influences GroupEmotionalDynamics

### Scenario 5: Mood Fluctuation and Affective Cycles

**Description:** In this scenario, a #MoodTracker monitors #MoodVariations and #AffectiveCycles through #MoodChanges and #EmotionalRhythms. The tracker observes #MoodShifts, #AffectivePatterns, and #EmotionalFluctuations while understanding #MoodTriggers and #AffectiveStability to predict #EmotionalTrajectories.

**Elements:**

- **MoodTracker** (Entity): Person monitoring and understanding patterns in emotional states
- **MoodVariations** (Quality): Different levels and types of emotional states over time
- **AffectiveCycles** (State): Regular patterns of emotional change and fluctuation
- **MoodChanges** (Process): Transitions between different emotional states
- **EmotionalRhythms** (State): Predictable timing patterns in emotional experiences
- **MoodShifts** (Process): Notable alterations in overall emotional tone
- **AffectivePatterns** (State): Recognizable sequences of emotional states
- **EmotionalFluctuations** (Process): Variations in emotional intensity and quality
- **MoodTriggers** (Entity): Events or factors that initiate mood changes
- **AffectiveStability** (Quality): Consistency and predictability of emotional states
- **EmotionalTrajectories** (State): Predicted paths of emotional change over time

**Relations:**

- MoodTracker monitors MoodVariations and AffectiveCycles
- AffectiveCycles include MoodChanges and EmotionalRhythms
- MoodTracker observes MoodShifts and EmotionalFluctuations
- EmotionalFluctuations follow identifiable AffectivePatterns
- MoodTriggers cause MoodShifts and EmotionalFluctuations
- AffectiveStability influences predictability of AffectiveCycles
- AffectivePatterns enable prediction of EmotionalTrajectories

---



## Perception and Sensation

**Domain:** Psychological  
**Subdomain:** Perception and Sensation

### Scenario 1: Sensory Input Processing and Perceptual Organization

**Description:** In this scenario, a #Perceiver receives #SensoryStimuli through #SensoryChannels and engages in #PerceptualProcessing to organize sensory information into #PerceptualObjects and #SensoryPatterns. The perceiver uses #AttentionalFocus and #PerceptualFiltering to create #OrganizedExperience from complex #SensoryInput.


**Elements:**

- **Perceiver** (Entity): Person actively processing and organizing sensory information
- **SensoryStimuli** (Entity): Environmental information detected by sensory organs
- **SensoryChannels** (Entity): Different modalities for receiving information (vision, hearing, touch, etc.)
- **PerceptualProcessing** (Process): Active organization and interpretation of sensory input
- **PerceptualObjects** (Entity): Organized units of perceptual experience (objects, sounds, textures)
- **SensoryPatterns** (Entity): Recurring arrangements or sequences in sensory information
- **AttentionalFocus** (Process): Selective concentration on particular aspects of sensory input
- **PerceptualFiltering** (Process): Screening and selection of relevant sensory information
- **OrganizedExperience** (State): Coherent perceptual understanding of environmental input
- **SensoryInput** (Entity): Raw information received through sensory systems

**Relations:**

- Perceiver receives SensoryStimuli through multiple SensoryChannels
- Perceiver engages in PerceptualProcessing of SensoryInput
- PerceptualProcessing organizes stimuli into PerceptualObjects and SensoryPatterns
- AttentionalFocus directs PerceptualProcessing toward relevant information
- PerceptualFiltering eliminates irrelevant SensoryStimuli
- PerceptualProcessing creates OrganizedExperience from SensoryInput
- SensoryPatterns emerge from organized PerceptualObjects

### Scenario 2: Perceptual Thresholds and Sensitivity Variations

**Description:** In this scenario, a #SensoryMonitor experiences varying #PerceptualThresholds and #SensitivityLevels across different #SensoryModalities, recognizing #DetectionLimits and #DiscriminationAbilities. The monitor understands #SensoryAdaptation and #PerceptualChanges that affect #SensoryAwareness and #PerceptualAccuracy.


**Elements:**

- **SensoryMonitor** (Entity): Person assessing and monitoring their own sensory capabilities
- **PerceptualThresholds** (Quality): Minimum levels of stimulation required for detection
- **SensitivityLevels** (Quality): Degrees of responsiveness to sensory stimulation
- **SensoryModalities** (Entity): Different types of sensory experience (visual, auditory, tactile, etc.)
- **DetectionLimits** (Quality): Boundaries of what can be sensed or perceived
- **DiscriminationAbilities** (Quality): Capacity to distinguish between similar stimuli
- **SensoryAdaptation** (Process): Adjustment of sensitivity based on exposure levels
- **PerceptualChanges** (Process): Alterations in sensory experience over time
- **SensoryAwareness** (State): Consciousness of one's own sensory capabilities and limitations
- **PerceptualAccuracy** (Quality): Precision and reliability of sensory detection and discrimination

**Relations:**

- SensoryMonitor experiences PerceptualThresholds across SensoryModalities
- Different SensoryModalities have distinct SensitivityLevels and DetectionLimits
- SensoryMonitor assesses DiscriminationAbilities within each modality
- SensoryAdaptation causes PerceptualChanges in SensitivityLevels
- SensoryAwareness includes understanding of personal PerceptualThresholds
- PerceptualAccuracy depends on SensitivityLevels and DiscriminationAbilities
- PerceptualChanges affect overall SensoryAwareness

### Scenario 3: Perceptual Illusions and Interpretation Errors

**Description:** In this scenario, a #PerceptualExplorer encounters #PerceptualIllusions and #SensoryMisinterpretations where #SensoryEvidence conflicts with #ActualReality. The explorer investigates #PerceptualDistortions and #InterpretationErrors that reveal #PerceptualMechanisms and #CognitiveInfluences on sensory experience.


**Elements:**

- **PerceptualExplorer** (Entity): Person investigating and understanding perceptual phenomena and errors
- **PerceptualIllusions** (Entity): Systematic misperceptions that differ from physical reality
- **SensoryMisinterpretations** (Process): Incorrect understanding of sensory information
- **SensoryEvidence** (Entity): Information provided by sensory systems
- **ActualReality** (Entity): Objective physical conditions independent of perception
- **PerceptualDistortions** (Process): Systematic alterations in sensory experience
- **InterpretationErrors** (Process): Mistakes in understanding sensory information
- **PerceptualMechanisms** (Process): Underlying systems that organize sensory experience
- **CognitiveInfluences** (Entity): Mental factors that affect perceptual interpretation

**Relations:**

- PerceptualExplorer encounters PerceptualIllusions and SensoryMisinterpretations
- PerceptualIllusions create discrepancies between SensoryEvidence and ActualReality
- SensoryMisinterpretations result from PerceptualDistortions and InterpretationErrors
- PerceptualDistortions reveal underlying PerceptualMechanisms
- CognitiveInfluences contribute to InterpretationErrors
- PerceptualMechanisms can systematically alter SensoryEvidence
- InterpretationErrors demonstrate interaction between perception and cognition

### Scenario 4: Sensory Integration and Cross-Modal Processing

**Description:** In this scenario, a #SensoryIntegrator combines #MultiSensoryInputs through #CrossModalProcessing to create #IntegratedPerceptions and #UnifiedSensoryExperience. The integrator manages #SensoryConflicts and #ModalityInteractions while achieving #PerceptualCoherence through #SensoryBinding and #MultimodalIntegration.

**Elements:**

- **SensoryIntegrator** (Entity): Person combining information from multiple sensory modalities
- **MultiSensoryInputs** (Entity): Simultaneous information from different sensory channels
- **CrossModalProcessing** (Process): Integration of information across sensory modalities
- **IntegratedPerceptions** (Entity): Unified sensory experiences combining multiple modalities
- **UnifiedSensoryExperience** (State): Coherent perception drawing from multiple senses
- **SensoryConflicts** (Entity): Contradictory information from different sensory modalities
- **ModalityInteractions** (Process): Ways different sensory channels influence each other
- **PerceptualCoherence** (Quality): Consistency and unity in multi-sensory experience
- **SensoryBinding** (Process): Linking related information from different sensory channels
- **MultimodalIntegration** (Process): Systematic combination of cross-modal information

**Relations:**

- SensoryIntegrator receives MultiSensoryInputs for processing
- CrossModalProcessing combines information from different sensory channels
- CrossModalProcessing creates IntegratedPerceptions
- IntegratedPerceptions contribute to UnifiedSensoryExperience
- SensoryIntegrator resolves SensoryConflicts between modalities
- ModalityInteractions influence CrossModalProcessing
- SensoryBinding enables PerceptualCoherence
- MultimodalIntegration produces unified UnifiedSensoryExperience

### Scenario 5: Attention and Perceptual Selection

**Description:** In this scenario, an #AttentionController directs #SelectiveAttention toward #RelevantStimuli while filtering #IrrelevantInformation through #AttentionalFiltering. The controller manages #AttentionalCapacity and #FocusControl to optimize #PerceptualSelection and maintain #AttentionalSustainment despite #DistractingElements.

**Elements:**

- **AttentionController** (Entity): Person managing and directing attentional resources
- **SelectiveAttention** (Process): Focusing on specific sensory information while ignoring others
- **RelevantStimuli** (Entity): Sensory information important for current goals or tasks
- **IrrelevantInformation** (Entity): Sensory input not needed for current objectives
- **AttentionalFiltering** (Process): Screening out unimportant sensory information
- **AttentionalCapacity** (Quality): Limited cognitive resources available for attention
- **FocusControl** (Process): Deliberate direction and maintenance of attention
- **PerceptualSelection** (Process): Choosing which sensory information receives processing
- **AttentionalSustainment** (Process): Maintaining focus over extended time periods
- **DistractingElements** (Entity): Competing stimuli that draw attention away from targets

**Relations:**

- AttentionController directs SelectiveAttention toward RelevantStimuli
- SelectiveAttention uses AttentionalFiltering to exclude IrrelevantInformation
- AttentionController manages limited AttentionalCapacity
- FocusControl optimizes PerceptualSelection of important information
- PerceptualSelection prioritizes RelevantStimuli over DistractingElements
- AttentionalSustainment maintains SelectiveAttention over time
- DistractingElements challenge AttentionalSustainment and FocusControl

---


## Needs and Drives and Motivations

**Domain:** Psychological  
**Subdomain:** Needs and Drives and Motivations

### Scenario 1: Basic Need Recognition and Drive Satisfaction

**Description:** In this scenario, a #MotivatedAgent experiences #BasicNeeds and #BiologicalDrives that create #MotivationalStates directing behavior toward #NeedSatisfaction. The agent recognizes #DriveSignals and engages in #GoalDirectedBehavior to achieve #DriveReduction and restore #HomeostasisBalance.


**Elements:**

- **MotivatedAgent** (Entity): Person experiencing and responding to motivational forces
- **BasicNeeds** (Entity): Fundamental requirements for survival and wellbeing (hunger, thirst, safety, etc.)
- **BiologicalDrives** (Entity): Internal forces that energize behavior toward need satisfaction
- **MotivationalStates** (State): Internal conditions that direct and energize behavior
- **NeedSatisfaction** (Process): Fulfillment of basic requirements through appropriate actions
- **DriveSignals** (Entity): Internal cues indicating need states and motivational pressure
- **GoalDirectedBehavior** (Process): Actions specifically aimed at achieving need satisfaction
- **DriveReduction** (Process): Decrease in motivational pressure following need satisfaction
- **HomeostasisBalance** (State): Optimal internal conditions maintained through need satisfaction

**Relations:**

- MotivatedAgent experiences BasicNeeds that generate BiologicalDrives
- BiologicalDrives create MotivationalStates that direct behavior
- MotivatedAgent recognizes DriveSignals indicating need states
- DriveSignals motivate GoalDirectedBehavior toward NeedSatisfaction
- NeedSatisfaction leads to DriveReduction
- DriveReduction restores HomeostasisBalance
- HomeostasisBalance reduces MotivationalStates until new needs emerge

### Scenario 2: Psychological Motivations and Achievement Drives

**Description:** In this scenario, an #Achiever pursues #PsychologicalGoals driven by #AchievementMotivation and #CompetencyNeeds. The achiever engages in #SkillDevelopment and #PerformanceImprovement while seeking #Recognition and #SelfActualization through #AccomplishmentPursuit and #MasteryOrientation.

**Elements:**

- **Achiever** (Entity): Person motivated by achievement and competency goals
- **PsychologicalGoals** (Entity): Objectives related to personal growth, competence, and self-realization
- **AchievementMotivation** (Entity): Drive to accomplish challenging tasks and reach standards of excellence
- **CompetencyNeeds** (Entity): Requirements for feeling capable and effective
- **SkillDevelopment** (Process): Improvement of abilities and expertise
- **PerformanceImprovement** (Process): Enhancement of task execution and outcomes
- **Recognition** (Entity): Acknowledgment and appreciation from others for achievements
- **SelfActualization** (Process): Realization of personal potential and authentic self-expression
- **AccomplishmentPursuit** (Process): Active efforts to achieve significant goals
- **MasteryOrientation** (Quality): Focus on learning and skill development rather than just outcomes

**Relations:**

- Achiever pursues PsychologicalGoals driven by AchievementMotivation
- AchievementMotivation emerges from CompetencyNeeds
- Achiever engages in SkillDevelopment and PerformanceImprovement
- AccomplishmentPursuit involves both SkillDevelopment and seeking Recognition
- MasteryOrientation guides approach to SkillDevelopment
- PerformanceImprovement serves both CompetencyNeeds and Recognition seeking
- SelfActualization emerges from successful AccomplishmentPursuit

### Scenario 3: Social Motivations and Relationship Drives

**Description:** In this scenario, a #SocialSeeker is motivated by #BelongingNeeds and #RelationshipDrives to form #SocialConnections and maintain #InterpersonalBonds. The seeker engages in #SocialApproachBehavior and #RelationshipBuilding while seeking #SocialAcceptance and #EmotionalIntimacy.


**Elements:**

- **SocialSeeker** (Entity): Person motivated by social connection and belonging needs
- **BelongingNeeds** (Entity): Fundamental requirements for social inclusion and group membership
- **RelationshipDrives** (Entity): Motivational forces toward forming and maintaining interpersonal connections
- **SocialConnections** (Entity): Bonds and relationships formed with other people
- **InterpersonalBonds** (Relation): Emotional and social ties between individuals
- **SocialApproachBehavior** (Process): Actions aimed at initiating social contact and connection
- **RelationshipBuilding** (Process): Development and strengthening of interpersonal bonds
- **SocialAcceptance** (Entity): Being welcomed and valued by others or groups
- **EmotionalIntimacy** (State): Deep emotional connection and closeness with others

**Relations:**

- SocialSeeker is motivated by BelongingNeeds and RelationshipDrives
- BelongingNeeds generate motivation for SocialConnections
- RelationshipDrives energize SocialApproachBehavior
- SocialApproachBehavior initiates RelationshipBuilding processes
- RelationshipBuilding creates InterpersonalBonds and SocialConnections
- SocialConnections provide SocialAcceptance
- InterpersonalBonds can develop into EmotionalIntimacy
- SocialAcceptance and EmotionalIntimacy satisfy BelongingNeeds

### Scenario 4: Intrinsic Motivation and Self-Determined Behavior

**Description:** In this scenario, a #AutonomousAgent engages in #IntrinsicallyMotivatedBehavior driven by #InternalRewards and #PersonalInterests rather than #ExternalPressures. The agent experiences #AutonomousSatisfaction and #IntrinsicFulfillment through #SelfDirectedActivities and #PersonallyMeaningfulPursuits that align with #InternalValues.

**Elements:**

- **AutonomousAgent** (Entity): Person motivated by internal rather than external factors
- **IntrinsicallyMotivatedBehavior** (Process): Actions driven by internal satisfaction rather than external rewards
- **InternalRewards** (Entity): Personal satisfaction and enjoyment derived from activities
- **PersonalInterests** (Entity): Topics, activities, or domains that naturally attract attention
- **ExternalPressures** (Entity): Outside forces pushing toward particular behaviors
- **AutonomousSatisfaction** (State): Fulfillment from self-directed choices and actions
- **IntrinsicFulfillment** (State): Deep satisfaction from internally motivated activities
- **SelfDirectedActivities** (Entity): Pursuits chosen based on personal preference rather than obligation
- **PersonallyMeaningfulPursuits** (Entity): Activities that align with individual values and interests
- **InternalValues** (Entity): Personal principles and beliefs that guide behavior

**Relations:**

- AutonomousAgent engages in IntrinsicallyMotivatedBehavior
- IntrinsicallyMotivatedBehavior driven by InternalRewards and PersonalInterests
- AutonomousAgent resists ExternalPressures in favor of internal motivation
- SelfDirectedActivities generate AutonomousSatisfaction
- PersonallyMeaningfulPursuits create IntrinsicFulfillment
- PersonalInterests guide selection of SelfDirectedActivities
- InternalValues determine what constitutes PersonallyMeaningfulPursuits

### Scenario 5: Motivational Conflict and Drive Competition

**Description:** In this scenario, a #ConflictedIndividual experiences #MotivationalConflicts between #CompetingDrives and #ConflictingGoals. The individual faces #ApproachAvoidanceConflicts and #MultipleMotivations that create #MotivationalTension and require #ConflictResolution through #PrioritySelection and #MotivationalCompromise.

**Elements:**

- **ConflictedIndividual** (Entity): Person experiencing simultaneous competing motivations
- **MotivationalConflicts** (State): Situations where different drives pull in opposing directions
- **CompetingDrives** (Entity): Different motivational forces that cannot be satisfied simultaneously
- **ConflictingGoals** (Entity): Objectives that are mutually exclusive or contradictory
- **ApproachAvoidanceConflicts** (Entity): Situations where same target has both attractive and repulsive qualities
- **MultipleMotivations** (Entity): Several different drives active at the same time
- **MotivationalTension** (State): Psychological stress from unresolved motivational conflicts
- **ConflictResolution** (Process): Methods for resolving competing motivational demands
- **PrioritySelection** (Process): Choosing which motivations take precedence
- **MotivationalCompromise** (Process): Finding solutions that partially satisfy multiple drives

**Relations:**

- ConflictedIndividual experiences MotivationalConflicts between CompetingDrives
- CompetingDrives create ConflictingGoals that cannot be pursued simultaneously
- ApproachAvoidanceConflicts arise from mixed motivations toward same target
- MultipleMotivations generate MotivationalTension
- ConflictedIndividual engages in ConflictResolution to manage tension
- ConflictResolution involves PrioritySelection among competing drives
- MotivationalCompromise provides alternative to PrioritySelection

---


## Subjective Experience of the Body and Environment

**Domain:** Psychological  
**Subdomain:** Subjective Experience of the Body and Environment

### Scenario 1: Embodied Awareness and Proprioceptive Experience

**Description:** In this scenario, an #EmbodiedExperiencer maintains #BodyAwareness through #ProprioceptiveMonitoring and #InteroceptiveSensing, experiencing #SpatialEmbodiment and #BodySchemas. The experiencer integrates #PosturalInformation and #MovementSensations to maintain #EmbodiedPresence and #SomaticAwareness.

**Elements:**

- **EmbodiedExperiencer** (Entity): Person with conscious awareness of their bodily experience
- **BodyAwareness** (State): Conscious attention to bodily sensations and positioning
- **ProprioceptiveMonitoring** (Process): Sensing body position and movement through internal receptors
- **InteroceptiveSensing** (Process): Awareness of internal bodily signals and states
- **SpatialEmbodiment** (State): Sense of body position and orientation in space
- **BodySchemas** (Entity): Mental representations of body structure and capabilities
- **PosturalInformation** (Entity): Sensory data about body position and balance
- **MovementSensations** (Entity): Felt experience of bodily motion and position changes
- **EmbodiedPresence** (State): Feeling of being present in and through the body
- **SomaticAwareness** (State): Conscious attention to bodily sensations and feelings

**Relations:**

- EmbodiedExperiencer maintains BodyAwareness through ProprioceptiveMonitoring and InteroceptiveSensing
- ProprioceptiveMonitoring provides PosturalInformation and MovementSensations
- BodySchemas organize PosturalInformation into SpatialEmbodiment
- InteroceptiveSensing contributes to SomaticAwareness
- SpatialEmbodiment and SomaticAwareness create EmbodiedPresence
- MovementSensations update BodySchemas continuously
- EmbodiedPresence integrates all aspects of BodyAwareness

### Scenario 2: Environmental Presence and Atmospheric Awareness

**Description:** In this scenario, an #EnvironmentalPerceiver experiences #EnvironmentalPresence and #AtmosphericQualities through #AmbientAwareness and #SpatialSensing. The perceiver attunes to #EnvironmentalMoods and #SpatialAtmospheres while developing #PlaceSense and #EnvironmentalConnection.


**Elements:**

- **EnvironmentalPerceiver** (Entity): Person attuned to environmental qualities and atmospheric presence
- **EnvironmentalPresence** (State): Feeling of being situated within and connected to environment
- **AtmosphericQualities** (Quality): Felt characteristics of environmental spaces (warm, cold, welcoming, hostile)
- **AmbientAwareness** (Process): Perception of overall environmental context and mood
- **SpatialSensing** (Process): Awareness of spatial relationships and environmental structure
- **EnvironmentalMoods** (Quality): Emotional tones and feelings associated with places
- **SpatialAtmospheres** (Quality): Qualitative characteristics of spatial environments
- **PlaceSense** (State): Feeling of connection and belonging to specific locations
- **EnvironmentalConnection** (Relation): Bond between person and environmental setting

**Relations:**

- EnvironmentalPerceiver experiences EnvironmentalPresence through AmbientAwareness
- AmbientAwareness detects AtmosphericQualities and EnvironmentalMoods
- SpatialSensing contributes to perception of SpatialAtmospheres
- AtmosphericQualities and SpatialAtmospheres influence EnvironmentalPresence
- EnvironmentalMoods affect subjective experience of spaces
- PlaceSense emerges from positive EnvironmentalConnection
- EnvironmentalConnection strengthens through repeated EnvironmentalPresence

### Scenario 3: Embodied Emotions and Somatic Responses

**Description:** In this scenario, an #EmbodiedFeeler experiences #EmbodiedEmotions through #SomaticResponses and #BodyFeedback, recognizing #EmotionalEmbodiment and #PhysicalFeelingSates. The feeler attends to #GutFeelings and #BodyEmotions while integrating #SomaticInformation for #EmotionalAwareness.


**Elements:**

- **EmbodiedFeeler** (Entity): Person who experiences emotions through bodily sensations
- **EmbodiedEmotions** (Entity): Emotions experienced as physical sensations and bodily states
- **SomaticResponses** (Process): Physical reactions accompanying emotional states
- **BodyFeedback** (Entity): Physical sensations that provide information about emotional states
- **EmotionalEmbodiment** (State): Experience of emotions as integrated mind-body phenomena
- **PhysicalFeelingStates** (State): Bodily conditions associated with specific emotions
- **GutFeelings** (Entity): Intuitive emotional responses felt in the body
- **BodyEmotions** (Entity): Emotions primarily experienced through physical sensations
- **SomaticInformation** (Entity): Bodily data that contributes to emotional understanding
- **EmotionalAwareness** (State): Conscious recognition of emotional states through bodily experience

**Relations:**

- EmbodiedFeeler experiences EmbodiedEmotions through SomaticResponses
- SomaticResponses generate BodyFeedback about emotional states
- EmotionalEmbodiment integrates mental and PhysicalFeelingStates
- GutFeelings provide immediate SomaticInformation about situations
- BodyEmotions manifest as distinct PhysicalFeelingStates
- BodyFeedback contributes to EmotionalAwareness
- SomaticInformation enhances overall EmotionalAwareness

### Scenario 4: Temporal Embodiment and Duration Experience

**Description:** In this scenario, a #TemporalExperiencer perceives #SubjectiveTime and #DurationSensations through #EmbodiedTemporality and #BodyTimeAwareness. The experiencer notices #TemporalEmbodiment in #RhythmicProcesses and #TemporalFlow while understanding how #BodyRhythms and #PhysiologicalCycles influence #TimePerception.

**Elements:**

- **TemporalExperiencer** (Entity): Person experiencing time through bodily sensations and rhythms
- **SubjectiveTime** (State): Personal, felt experience of temporal flow and duration
- **DurationSensations** (Entity): Bodily felt sense of time passage and temporal intervals
- **EmbodiedTemporality** (State): Experience of time as mediated through bodily processes
- **BodyTimeAwareness** (State): Consciousness of temporal aspects of bodily experience
- **TemporalEmbodiment** (State): Integration of time perception with bodily awareness
- **RhythmicProcesses** (Process): Regular, cyclical bodily functions and movements
- **TemporalFlow** (State): Sense of time moving and progressing through embodied experience
- **BodyRhythms** (Entity): Natural cyclical patterns in bodily functions
- **PhysiologicalCycles** (Entity): Biological rhythms affecting temporal experience
- **TimePerception** (Process): Subjective awareness and interpretation of temporal duration

**Relations:**

- TemporalExperiencer perceives SubjectiveTime through EmbodiedTemporality
- EmbodiedTemporality includes DurationSensations and BodyTimeAwareness
- TemporalEmbodiment emerges from integration of bodily and temporal awareness
- RhythmicProcesses contribute to sense of TemporalFlow
- BodyRhythms and PhysiologicalCycles influence TimePerception
- DurationSensations vary with different PhysiologicalCycles
- BodyTimeAwareness enables recognition of TemporalEmbodiment

### Scenario 5: Comfort and Discomfort Experiences

**Description:** In this scenario, a #ComfortSeeker experiences #BodilyComfort and #PhysicalDiscomfort through #ComfortSensations and #DiscomfortSignals. The seeker engages in #ComfortSeeking behaviors and #DiscomfortAvoidance while understanding #ComfortFactors and #DiscomfortCauses that influence #BodyWellbeing and #PhysicalSatisfaction.

**Elements:**

- **ComfortSeeker** (Entity): Person pursuing physical comfort and avoiding discomfort
- **BodilyComfort** (State): Pleasant, satisfied physical sensations and conditions
- **PhysicalDiscomfort** (State): Unpleasant, aversive bodily sensations and conditions
- **ComfortSensations** (Entity): Pleasant bodily feelings indicating good physical conditions
- **DiscomfortSignals** (Entity): Unpleasant bodily feelings indicating problematic conditions
- **ComfortSeeking** (Process): Behaviors aimed at achieving pleasant physical states
- **DiscomfortAvoidance** (Process): Actions taken to prevent or eliminate unpleasant sensations
- **ComfortFactors** (Entity): Conditions and elements that promote physical comfort
- **DiscomfortCauses** (Entity): Factors that create unpleasant bodily experiences
- **BodyWellbeing** (State): Overall positive physical condition and satisfaction
- **PhysicalSatisfaction** (State): Contentment with bodily conditions and sensations

**Relations:**

- ComfortSeeker experiences BodilyComfort and PhysicalDiscomfort
- BodilyComfort manifests through ComfortSensations
- PhysicalDiscomfort manifests through DiscomfortSignals
- ComfortSeeker engages in ComfortSeeking to increase pleasant sensations
- DiscomfortAvoidance reduces PhysicalDiscomfort
- ComfortFactors promote BodilyComfort and BodyWellbeing
- DiscomfortCauses generate PhysicalDiscomfort
- BodyWellbeing contributes to overall PhysicalSatisfaction

# Representational Domain

## Information Structures

**Domain:** Representational  
**Subdomain:** Information Structures

### Scenario 1: Data Organization and Categorical Systems

**Description:** In this scenario, an #InformationOrganizer creates #OrganizationalSystems by establishing #CategoryStructures and #ClassificationSchemes to manage #DataCollections. The organizer uses #TaxonomicPrinciples and #HierarchicalOrganization to create #LogicalGroupings and enable efficient #InformationRetrieval.

**Elements:**

- **InformationOrganizer** (Entity): Person creating systematic structures for information management
- **OrganizationalSystems** (Entity): Structured frameworks for organizing and accessing information
- **CategoryStructures** (Entity): Systematic groupings based on shared characteristics
- **ClassificationSchemes** (Entity): Formal systems for organizing information into categories
- **DataCollections** (Entity): Sets of information requiring organization
- **TaxonomicPrinciples** (Entity): Rules and criteria for creating categorical hierarchies
- **HierarchicalOrganization** (State): Multi-level structures with nested categories
- **LogicalGroupings** (Entity): Categories based on rational or systematic criteria
- **InformationRetrieval** (Process): Accessing specific information from organized systems

**Relations:**

- InformationOrganizer creates OrganizationalSystems for DataCollections
- OrganizationalSystems employ CategoryStructures and ClassificationSchemes
- CategoryStructures follow TaxonomicPrinciples
- TaxonomicPrinciples guide HierarchicalOrganization
- ClassificationSchemes create LogicalGroupings of information
- HierarchicalOrganization facilitates efficient InformationRetrieval
- LogicalGroupings enhance systematic InformationRetrieval

### Scenario 2: Relational Structures and Network Organization

**Description:** In this scenario, a #NetworkBuilder constructs #RelationalNetworks and #ConnectionSystems by identifying #InformationNodes and establishing #LinkagePatterns. The builder creates #AssociativeStructures and #NetworkTopologies that represent #InterconnectedRelationships and enable #PathwayNavigation through information spaces.

**Elements:**

- **NetworkBuilder** (Entity): Person creating relational and network-based information structures
- **RelationalNetworks** (Entity): Information structures organized around relationships and connections
- **ConnectionSystems** (Entity): Networks of linked information elements
- **InformationNodes** (Entity): Individual information elements that can be connected to others
- **LinkagePatterns** (State): Ways in which information elements are connected
- **AssociativeStructures** (Entity): Organizations based on meaningful associations between elements
- **NetworkTopologies** (Entity): Overall patterns of connections within networks
- **InterconnectedRelationships** (Relation): Mutual connections between information elements
- **PathwayNavigation** (Process): Moving through networks by following connections

**Relations:**

- NetworkBuilder constructs RelationalNetworks and ConnectionSystems
- RelationalNetworks composed of InformationNodes connected through LinkagePatterns
- NetworkBuilder establishes InterconnectedRelationships between nodes
- LinkagePatterns create AssociativeStructures within networks
- AssociativeStructures form specific NetworkTopologies
- NetworkTopologies enable PathwayNavigation through information
- PathwayNavigation utilizes InterconnectedRelationships

### Scenario 3: Sequential Structures and Procedural Organization

**Description:** In this scenario, a #ProcessOrganizer develops #SequentialStructures and #ProceduralFrameworks by ordering #InformationSequences and creating #StepByStepOrganization. The organizer establishes #TemporalOrdering and #LogicalProgression to support #ProcessualNavigation and #SequentialAccess of information.

**Elements:**

- **ProcessOrganizer** (Entity): Person creating sequential and procedural information structures
- **SequentialStructures** (Entity): Information organized in temporal or logical order
- **ProceduralFrameworks** (Entity): Systematic organizations for step-based processes
- **InformationSequences** (Entity): Ordered series of related information elements
- **StepByStepOrganization** (State): Arrangement of information in discrete sequential steps
- **TemporalOrdering** (Quality): Organization based on time-based sequences
- **LogicalProgression** (Quality): Organization based on rational or causal sequences
- **ProcessualNavigation** (Process): Moving through information following procedural steps
- **SequentialAccess** (Process): Accessing information in predetermined order

**Relations:**

- ProcessOrganizer develops SequentialStructures and ProceduralFrameworks
- SequentialStructures organize InformationSequences in order
- ProceduralFrameworks employ StepByStepOrganization
- InformationSequences follow TemporalOrdering or LogicalProgression
- StepByStepOrganization enables ProcessualNavigation
- TemporalOrdering and LogicalProgression guide SequentialAccess
- ProcessualNavigation utilizes established ProceduralFrameworks

### Scenario 4: Adaptive Information Systems and Dynamic Reorganization

**Description:** In this scenario, an #AdaptiveSystemManager creates #DynamicInformationSystems that automatically adjust #OrganizationalPatterns based on #UsageAnalytics and #AccessPatterns. The manager implements #AdaptiveAlgorithms and #SystemLearning to enable #AutomaticReorganization and #ContextualAdaptation that optimize #InformationAccessibility and #UserEfficiency.

**Elements:**

- **AdaptiveSystemManager** (Entity): Person designing systems that automatically adjust to usage patterns
- **DynamicInformationSystems** (Entity): Information structures that modify themselves based on usage
- **OrganizationalPatterns** (State): Current arrangements of information elements
- **UsageAnalytics** (Entity): Data about how information is accessed and used
- **AccessPatterns** (State): Regular ways users interact with information
- **AdaptiveAlgorithms** (Process): Computational methods for automatic system adjustment
- **SystemLearning** (Process): Automated improvement based on usage experience
- **AutomaticReorganization** (Process): Self-modification of information structures
- **ContextualAdaptation** (Process): Adjustment based on situational factors
- **InformationAccessibility** (Quality): Ease of finding and retrieving information
- **UserEfficiency** (Quality): Speed and effectiveness of information interaction

**Relations:**

- AdaptiveSystemManager creates DynamicInformationSystems with adaptive capabilities
- DynamicInformationSystems monitor UsageAnalytics and AccessPatterns
- AdaptiveAlgorithms analyze UsageAnalytics to identify optimization opportunities
- SystemLearning enables continuous improvement of OrganizationalPatterns
- AutomaticReorganization modifies structures based on SystemLearning
- ContextualAdaptation adjusts organization for specific situations
- DynamicInformationSystems optimize InformationAccessibility and UserEfficiency

### Scenario 5: Cross-Modal Information Integration and Unified Access

**Description:** In this scenario, a #MultimodalIntegrator combines #HeterogeneousDataSources containing #TextualInformation, #VisualData, #AudioContent, and #SpatialInformation into #UnifiedInformationStructures. The integrator uses #CrossModalLinking and #SemanticAlignment to create #IntegratedAccessSystems that enable #MultimodalRetrieval and #CoherentInformationExperience.

**Elements:**

- **MultimodalIntegrator** (Entity): Person combining different types of information into unified systems
- **HeterogeneousDataSources** (Entity): Different types of information repositories
- **TextualInformation** (Entity): Written or linguistic content
- **VisualData** (Entity): Images, graphics, and visual content
- **AudioContent** (Entity): Sound, speech, and audio information
- **SpatialInformation** (Entity): Location and geographic data
- **UnifiedInformationStructures** (Entity): Integrated systems combining multiple data types
- **CrossModalLinking** (Process): Creating connections between different information types
- **SemanticAlignment** (Process): Ensuring consistent meaning across modalities
- **IntegratedAccessSystems** (Entity): Unified interfaces for multimodal information
- **MultimodalRetrieval** (Process): Searching across different information types simultaneously
- **CoherentInformationExperience** (State): Seamless interaction with diverse information types

**Relations:**

- MultimodalIntegrator combines HeterogeneousDataSources
- HeterogeneousDataSources contain TextualInformation, VisualData, AudioContent, and SpatialInformation
- MultimodalIntegrator employs CrossModalLinking between different data types
- SemanticAlignment ensures consistency across information modalities
- CrossModalLinking and SemanticAlignment create UnifiedInformationStructures
- UnifiedInformationStructures enable IntegratedAccessSystems
- IntegratedAccessSystems support MultimodalRetrieval
- MultimodalRetrieval provides CoherentInformationExperience

---


## Media and Digital Systems

**Domain:** Representational  
**Subdomain:** Media and Digital Systems

### Scenario 1: Digital Content Creation and Multimedia Integration

**Description:** In this scenario, a #DigitalCreator produces #DigitalContent using #MultimediaElements and #ContentCreationTools to develop #IntegratedMedia experiences. The creator combines #TextElements, #VisualComponents, #AudioElements, and #InteractiveFeatures through #MediaIntegration to create #DigitalProducts.

**Elements:**

- **DigitalCreator** (Entity): Person producing content using digital media technologies
- **DigitalContent** (Entity): Information and media produced using digital technologies
- **MultimediaElements** (Entity): Various types of media content (text, image, audio, video)
- **ContentCreationTools** (Entity): Software and technologies for producing digital content
- **IntegratedMedia** (Entity): Combined multimedia experiences
- **TextElements** (Entity): Written or textual content components
- **VisualComponents** (Entity): Images, graphics, and visual design elements
- **AudioElements** (Entity): Sound, music, and audio content
- **InteractiveFeatures** (Entity): Elements that enable user interaction and engagement
- **MediaIntegration** (Process): Combining different media types into cohesive experiences
- **DigitalProducts** (Entity): Final multimedia creations

**Relations:**

- DigitalCreator produces DigitalContent using ContentCreationTools
- DigitalContent incorporates MultimediaElements
- MultimediaElements include TextElements, VisualComponents, AudioElements, and InteractiveFeatures
- DigitalCreator employs MediaIntegration to combine elements
- MediaIntegration creates IntegratedMedia experiences
- IntegratedMedia becomes final DigitalProducts
- ContentCreationTools enable effective MediaIntegration

### Scenario 2: Digital Information Processing and Data Management

**Description:** In this scenario, a #DataProcessor manages #DigitalInformation through #DataProcessingSystems and #InformationManagement techniques. The processor handles #DataInput, #DataTransformation, and #DataOutput while ensuring #DataIntegrity and #SystemEfficiency through #DigitalWorkflows.


**Elements:**

- **DataProcessor** (Entity): Person managing and processing digital information
- **DigitalInformation** (Entity): Information stored and processed in digital formats
- **DataProcessingSystems** (Entity): Technologies for handling and transforming digital data
- **InformationManagement** (Process): Systematic handling of digital information
- **DataInput** (Process): Entry of information into digital systems
- **DataTransformation** (Process): Modification and processing of digital information
- **DataOutput** (Process): Extraction of processed information from systems
- **DataIntegrity** (Quality): Accuracy and reliability of digital information
- **SystemEfficiency** (Quality): Optimal performance of digital processing systems
- **DigitalWorkflows** (Process): Systematic procedures for digital information handling

**Relations:**

- DataProcessor manages DigitalInformation through DataProcessingSystems
- InformationManagement involves DataInput, DataTransformation, and DataOutput
- DataProcessingSystems handle DigitalInformation processing
- DataProcessor ensures DataIntegrity during processing
- DigitalWorkflows optimize SystemEfficiency
- DataTransformation modifies DigitalInformation while maintaining DataIntegrity
- SystemEfficiency depends on effective DigitalWorkflows

### Scenario 3: Digital Communication and Interactive Systems

**Description:** In this scenario, a #DigitalCommunicator uses #DigitalPlatforms and #InteractiveSystems to facilitate #OnlineCommunication and #DigitalInteraction. The communicator employs #CommunicationTools and #InterfaceDesign to create #UserExperiences that enable #DigitalCollaboration and #VirtualEngagement.


**Elements:**

- **DigitalCommunicator** (Entity): Person facilitating communication through digital technologies
- **DigitalPlatforms** (Entity): Online systems that enable digital communication and interaction
- **InteractiveSystems** (Entity): Technologies that support user interaction and engagement
- **OnlineCommunication** (Process): Communication conducted through digital networks
- **DigitalInteraction** (Process): Engagement between users through digital interfaces
- **CommunicationTools** (Entity): Software and features that enable digital communication
- **InterfaceDesign** (Process): Creation of user interfaces for digital systems
- **UserExperiences** (Entity): Overall experiences people have when using digital systems
- **DigitalCollaboration** (Process): Cooperative work conducted through digital platforms
- **VirtualEngagement** (Process): Participation in digital environments and activities

**Relations:**

- DigitalCommunicator uses DigitalPlatforms and InteractiveSystems
- DigitalPlatforms enable OnlineCommunication and DigitalInteraction
- CommunicationTools facilitate OnlineCommunication
- InterfaceDesign shapes UserExperiences
- InteractiveSystems support DigitalCollaboration and VirtualEngagement
- UserExperiences influence effectiveness of DigitalInteraction
- DigitalCollaboration utilizes CommunicationTools and DigitalPlatforms

### Scenario 4: Digital Preservation and Archive Management

**Description:** In this scenario, a #DigitalArchivist manages #DigitalPreservation of #CulturalArtifacts and #DigitalHeritage through #ArchivalSystems and #PreservationStrategies. The archivist implements #LongTermStorage, #FormatMigration, and #MetadataManagement to ensure #DigitalLongevity and enable #FutureAccess while maintaining #ArchivalIntegrity.

**Elements:**

- **DigitalArchivist** (Entity): Person responsible for long-term digital preservation
- **DigitalPreservation** (Process): Systematic protection of digital materials over time
- **CulturalArtifacts** (Entity): Digital representations of culturally significant items
- **DigitalHeritage** (Entity): Digital materials with historical or cultural value
- **ArchivalSystems** (Entity): Technologies designed for long-term digital storage
- **PreservationStrategies** (Process): Planned approaches to maintaining digital materials
- **LongTermStorage** (Process): Secure storage designed for extended time periods
- **FormatMigration** (Process): Converting digital materials to current formats
- **MetadataManagement** (Process): Organizing descriptive information about digital materials
- **DigitalLongevity** (Quality): Ability of digital materials to remain accessible over time
- **FutureAccess** (Quality): Ensuring digital materials remain usable by future users
- **ArchivalIntegrity** (Quality): Maintaining authenticity and completeness of preserved materials

**Relations:**

- DigitalArchivist manages DigitalPreservation of CulturalArtifacts and DigitalHeritage
- DigitalPreservation utilizes ArchivalSystems and PreservationStrategies
- PreservationStrategies include LongTermStorage and FormatMigration
- MetadataManagement supports organization of preserved materials
- LongTermStorage and FormatMigration ensure DigitalLongevity
- DigitalPreservation enables FutureAccess to materials
- ArchivalSystems maintain ArchivalIntegrity throughout preservation

### Scenario 5: Human-Computer Interface Adaptation and Accessibility

**Description:** In this scenario, an #InterfaceDesigner creates #AdaptiveInterfaces and #AccessibilityFeatures that adjust to #UserCapabilities and #AccessibilityNeeds. The designer implements #PersonalizationSystems and #AssistiveTechnologies to provide #InclusiveDesign and #UniversalAccess while ensuring #UsabilityOptimization and #BarrierRemoval.

**Elements:**

- **InterfaceDesigner** (Entity): Person creating adaptive and accessible digital interfaces
- **AdaptiveInterfaces** (Entity): User interfaces that adjust to individual user needs
- **AccessibilityFeatures** (Entity): Design elements that support users with disabilities
- **UserCapabilities** (Entity): Individual abilities and limitations of system users
- **AccessibilityNeeds** (Entity): Specific requirements for barrier-free system use
- **PersonalizationSystems** (Entity): Technologies that customize interfaces for individual users
- **AssistiveTechnologies** (Entity): Tools that help users with disabilities interact with systems
- **InclusiveDesign** (Process): Creating interfaces usable by people with diverse abilities
- **UniversalAccess** (Quality): Ability for all users to access and use systems effectively
- **UsabilityOptimization** (Process): Improving ease and efficiency of system use
- **BarrierRemoval** (Process): Eliminating obstacles to system access and use

**Relations:**

- InterfaceDesigner creates AdaptiveInterfaces with AccessibilityFeatures
- AdaptiveInterfaces adjust to UserCapabilities and AccessibilityNeeds
- PersonalizationSystems enable customization for individual UserCapabilities
- AssistiveTechnologies support users with specific AccessibilityNeeds
- InclusiveDesign principles guide creation of AdaptiveInterfaces
- AccessibilityFeatures and AssistiveTechnologies enable UniversalAccess
- UsabilityOptimization and BarrierRemoval enhance system accessibility

## Formal Systems and Abstract Representations

**Domain:** Representational  
**Subdomain:** Formal Systems and Abstract Representations

### Scenario 1: Mathematical Systems and Logical Structures

**Description:** In this scenario, a #MathematicalThinker works with #MathematicalSystems and #LogicalStructures, using #FormalNotations and #SymbolicRepresentations to express #AbstractConcepts and #QuantitativeRelationships. The thinker applies #MathematicalOperations and #LogicalRules to derive #FormalConclusions and solve #AbstractProblems.

**Elements:**

- **MathematicalThinker** (Entity): Person working with formal mathematical and logical systems
- **MathematicalSystems** (Entity): Formal frameworks for quantitative and abstract reasoning
- **LogicalStructures** (Entity): Systematic frameworks for reasoning and inference
- **FormalNotations** (Entity): Symbolic systems for representing mathematical and logical concepts
- **SymbolicRepresentations** (Entity): Abstract symbols that represent concepts and relationships
- **AbstractConcepts** (Entity): Ideas that exist independent of specific concrete instances
- **QuantitativeRelationships** (Relation): Mathematical connections between quantities
- **MathematicalOperations** (Process): Formal procedures for manipulating mathematical expressions
- **LogicalRules** (Entity): Principles governing valid reasoning and inference
- **FormalConclusions** (Entity): Results derived through systematic application of formal rules
- **AbstractProblems** (Entity): Challenges requiring formal mathematical or logical solutions

**Relations:**

- MathematicalThinker works with MathematicalSystems and LogicalStructures
- MathematicalSystems use FormalNotations and SymbolicRepresentations
- SymbolicRepresentations express AbstractConcepts and QuantitativeRelationships
- MathematicalThinker applies MathematicalOperations following LogicalRules
- MathematicalOperations transform SymbolicRepresentations
- LogicalRules guide derivation of FormalConclusions
- FormalConclusions solve AbstractProblems

### Scenario 2: Theoretical Models and Systematic Frameworks

**Description:** In this scenario, a #ModelBuilder constructs #TheoreticalModels and #SystematicFrameworks using #AbstractModeling and #ConceptualStructures to represent #ComplexPhenomena. The builder develops #ModelComponents and #FrameworkElements that capture #EssentialRelationships and enable #TheoreticalPredictions.


**Elements:**

- **ModelBuilder** (Entity): Person creating theoretical models and systematic frameworks
- **TheoreticalModels** (Entity): Abstract representations of real-world phenomena
- **SystematicFrameworks** (Entity): Organized structures for understanding complex systems
- **AbstractModeling** (Process): Creation of simplified representations of complex phenomena
- **ConceptualStructures** (Entity): Organized systems of related concepts
- **ComplexPhenomena** (Entity): Multi-faceted real-world processes or systems
- **ModelComponents** (Entity): Elements that make up theoretical models
- **FrameworkElements** (Entity): Components of systematic frameworks
- **EssentialRelationships** (Relation): Key connections between model components
- **TheoreticalPredictions** (Entity): Forecasts derived from model applications

**Relations:**

- ModelBuilder constructs TheoreticalModels and SystematicFrameworks
- AbstractModeling creates representations of ComplexPhenomena
- TheoreticalModels composed of ModelComponents and ConceptualStructures
- SystematicFrameworks include FrameworkElements
- ModelComponents connected through EssentialRelationships
- TheoreticalModels enable TheoreticalPredictions
- EssentialRelationships determine predictive capabilities

### Scenario 3: Algorithmic Thinking and Computational Representations

**Description:** In this scenario, an #AlgorithmDesigner develops #AlgorithmicProcesses and #ComputationalModels using #SystematicProcedures and #LogicalSequences. The designer creates #StepWiseAlgorithms and #ComputationalLogic to solve #DefinedProblems through #AutomatableProcesses and #SystematicExecution.


**Elements:**

- **AlgorithmDesigner** (Entity): Person creating systematic computational procedures
- **AlgorithmicProcesses** (Process): Systematic step-by-step procedures for problem solving
- **ComputationalModels** (Entity): Abstract representations designed for computational processing
- **SystematicProcedures** (Process): Organized sequences of actions or operations
- **LogicalSequences** (Entity): Ordered steps following logical progression
- **StepWiseAlgorithms** (Entity): Procedures broken down into discrete, executable steps
- **ComputationalLogic** (Entity): Reasoning principles suitable for automated execution
- **DefinedProblems** (Entity): Well-specified challenges with clear solution criteria
- **AutomatableProcesses** (Process): Procedures that can be executed without human intervention
- **SystematicExecution** (Process): Carrying out procedures following established steps

**Relations:**

- AlgorithmDesigner develops AlgorithmicProcesses and ComputationalModels
- AlgorithmicProcesses employ SystematicProcedures and LogicalSequences
- StepWiseAlgorithms implement ComputationalLogic
- AlgorithmicProcesses designed to solve DefinedProblems
- SystematicProcedures enable AutomatableProcesses
- LogicalSequences guide SystematicExecution
- ComputationalModels support AutomatableProcesses

### Scenario 4: Rule System Evolution and Formal System Modification

**Description:** In this scenario, a #SystemEvolutionist modifies #ExistingFormalSystems through #RuleModification and #SystemExtension processes. The evolutionist analyzes #SystemLimitations and #ExpressiveConstraints to implement #RuleGeneralization, #SystemAdaptation, and #FormalSystemUpgrades that enhance #SystemCapabilities and maintain #LogicalConsistency.

**Elements:**

- **SystemEvolutionist** (Entity): Person modifying and extending formal systems
- **ExistingFormalSystems** (Entity): Established mathematical or logical frameworks
- **RuleModification** (Process): Changing existing rules within formal systems
- **SystemExtension** (Process): Adding new capabilities to formal systems
- **SystemLimitations** (Entity): Constraints that restrict formal system capabilities
- **ExpressiveConstraints** (Quality): Limits on what can be represented in the system
- **RuleGeneralization** (Process): Making rules more broadly applicable
- **SystemAdaptation** (Process): Adjusting systems for new applications
- **FormalSystemUpgrades** (Process): Systematic improvements to formal systems
- **SystemCapabilities** (Quality): Range of problems the system can address
- **LogicalConsistency** (Quality): Freedom from contradictions within the system

**Relations:**

- SystemEvolutionist modifies ExistingFormalSystems through RuleModification and SystemExtension
- SystemEvolutionist analyzes SystemLimitations and ExpressiveConstraints
- RuleGeneralization addresses identified SystemLimitations
- SystemAdaptation adjusts systems for expanded applications
- FormalSystemUpgrades implement systematic improvements
- RuleModification and SystemExtension enhance SystemCapabilities
- LogicalConsistency must be maintained throughout modifications

### Scenario 5: Abstraction Level Transitions and Multi-Level Representation

**Description:** In this scenario, an #AbstractionSpecialist works with #MultiLevelRepresentations by managing #AbstractionTransitions between #DetailedLevel, #IntermediateLevel, and #AbstractLevel representations. The specialist uses #LevelMapping and #AbstractionMechanisms to enable #LevelNavigation and #ScaleTransition while maintaining #RepresentationalCoherence across abstraction levels.

**Elements:**

- **AbstractionSpecialist** (Entity): Person managing multiple levels of abstraction in representations
- **MultiLevelRepresentations** (Entity): Systems with multiple levels of detail and abstraction
- **AbstractionTransitions** (Process): Movement between different levels of abstraction
- **DetailedLevel** (State): Highly specific, concrete representations
- **IntermediateLevel** (State): Moderate abstraction balancing detail and generality
- **AbstractLevel** (State): Highly general, conceptual representations
- **LevelMapping** (Process): Creating correspondences between abstraction levels
- **AbstractionMechanisms** (Process): Systematic methods for changing abstraction levels
- **LevelNavigation** (Process): Moving between different abstraction levels
- **ScaleTransition** (Process): Adjusting scope and granularity of representation
- **RepresentationalCoherence** (Quality): Consistency of meaning across abstraction levels

**Relations:**

- AbstractionSpecialist works with MultiLevelRepresentations
- MultiLevelRepresentations include DetailedLevel, IntermediateLevel, and AbstractLevel
- AbstractionSpecialist manages AbstractionTransitions between levels
- LevelMapping creates connections between different abstraction levels
- AbstractionMechanisms enable systematic LevelNavigation
- ScaleTransition adjusts granularity within AbstractionTransitions
- RepresentationalCoherence ensures consistent meaning across all levels
